# Text Elements
class SparseTable:
    def __init__(self, data, func=min):
        self.func = func
        self.k = self._log2(len(data))
        self.t = [[0] * self.k for _ in range(len(data))]
        self._build(data)

    def _log2(self, n):
        result = 0
        while n > 1:
            n >>= 1
            result += 1
        return result

    def _build(self, data):
        for i in range(len(data)):
            self.t[i][0] = data[i]

        for j in range(1, self.k):
            s = 1 << (j - 1)
            for i in range(len(data) - s):
                self.t[i][j] = self.func(self.t[i][j - 1], self.t[i + s][j - 1])

    def query(self, l, r):
        m = self._log2(r - l)
        return self.func(self.t[l][m], self.t[r - (1 << m)][m]) ^RCMiYkEO

template<typename T>
class SparseTable {
    typedef function<T(T, T)> Func;

    size_t k;
    vector<vector<T>> t;
    Func func;

public:
    template<typename It, typename F>
    SparseTable(It first, It last, F f) {
        auto n = std::distance(first, last);
        k = log2(n) + 1;
        func = f;
        t.resize(n);
        for (auto &r: t) {
            r.resize(k);
            r[0] = *first++;
        }
        build();
    }

    T query(size_t l, size_t r) {
        size_t m = log2(r - l);
        return func(t[l][m], t[r - (1 << m)][m]);
    }

private:
    size_t log2(size_t n) {
        size_t result = 0;
        while (n >>= 1)
            result++;
        return result;
    }

    void build() {
        for (size_t j = 1; j < k; ++j) {
            size_t s = 1 << (j - 1);
            for (size_t i = 0; i < t.size() - s; ++i)
                t[i][j] = func(t[i][j - 1], t[i + s][j - 1]);
        }
    }
}; ^5pjMrcOT
